Such editions are also <a href="/wiki/Public_domain" title="Public domain">public domain</a> in Canada because they fail to meet the minimum ‘threshold of originality’ to qualify for copyright as an ‘adaptation’. It may not be <a href="/wiki/Public_domain" title="Public domain">public domain</a> elsewhere, however. <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Les nuits d’été (Summer Nights)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Six mélodies avec un petit orchestre
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Berlioz,_Hector" title="Category:Berlioz, Hector">Berlioz, Hector</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Œuvre 7&#160;; H 81 (A and B)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IHB 46
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 songs:
<ol><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Villanelle,_H_82_(Berlioz,_Hector)" title="Villanelle, H 82 (Berlioz, Hector)">Villanelle</a></i>, H 82<br />mezzo-soprano or tenor
</li><li> <i>Le spectre de la rose</i>, H 83<br />mezzo-soprano or tenor (A), contralto (B)
</li><li> <i>Sur les lagunes: lamento</i>, H 84<br />mezzo-soprano or tenor (A), baritone, contralto, or mezzo-soprano (B)
</li><li> <i>Absence</i>, H 85<br />mezzo-soprano or tenor
</li><li> <i>Au cimitière: clair de lune</i>, H 86<br />mezzo-soprano or tenor (A), tenor (B)
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/L%E2%80%99%C3%AEle_inconnue,_H_87_(Berlioz,_Hector)" title="L’île inconnue, H 87 (Berlioz, Hector)" class="mw-redirect">L’île inconnue</a></i>: <i>barcarolle</i>, H 87<br />mezzo-soprano or tenor
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1840–41, orchestrated 1856
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1841 (H 81A) - Paris: Ad. Catelin &amp; Cie., Plate Ad.C. 872 &amp; Cie., 25 pages (to Richault after 1843)<br />1856 (H 81B) - Winterthur: J. Rieter-Biedermann, Plate 2, 72 pages
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Gautier,_Th%C3%A9ophile" title="Category:Gautier, Théophile">Théophile Gautier</a> (1811–1872)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>French
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bertin,_Louise" title="Category:Bertin, Louise">Louise Bertin</a> (voice and piano)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>30 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voice, piano (see comments); arranged for voice, orchestra
<dl><dd>2 flutes, oboe, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons, 3 horns, harp, strings
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Les_nuits_d%27%C3%A9t%C3%A9" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Les nuits d'été">Wikipedia article</a><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20071019225303/http://hector.ucdavis.edu/Berlioz2003/Works/H81A.html">voice and piano (H 81A)</a></span><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20071019225303/http://hector.ucdavis.edu/Berlioz2003/Works/H81B.html">voice and orchestra (H 81B)</a></span><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.lieder.net/lieder/assemble_texts.html?SongCycleId=72">The Lied, Art Song, and Choral Texts Archive</a></span><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.hberlioz.com/Libretti/Nuits.htm">Libretto (Berlioz Website)</a></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Publication_History">Publication History</span></h4>
<dl><dt>Voice and Piano
</dt></dl>
<ul><li>Paris: 1841, as Œuvre 7 - Ad. Catelin &amp; Cie., Plate Ad.C. 872 &amp; Cie., 25 pages (to Richault after 1843)
</li><li>Paris: 1863, included in <i>Collection de 32 Mélodies</i>: nos. 1–6
</li><li>Leipzig: <a href="/wiki/Breitkopf_und_H%C3%A4rtel" title="Breitkopf und Härtel">Breitkopf und Härtel</a>, n.d.(1904), as part of Hector Berlioz Werke (1900–07), Serie VII, Band XVII, edited by Charles Malherbe and Felix Weingartner
</li><li>Kassel: <a href="/wiki/B%C3%A4renreiter" title="Bärenreiter">Bärenreiter</a>, 2005, BA 5455, as part of <a href="/wiki/Hector_Berlioz,_New_Berlioz_Edition" title="Hector Berlioz, New Berlioz Edition" class="mw-redirect">New Berlioz Edition</a> (1967–2005), Volume 15, edited by Ian Rumbold
</li></ul>
<dl><dt>Voice and Orchestra
</dt></dl>
<ul><li>Paris: 1856 (full score, parts) - Winterthur: J. Rieter-Biedermann, Plate 2, 72 pages
</li><li>Leipzig: <a href="/wiki/Breitkopf_und_H%C3%A4rtel" title="Breitkopf und Härtel">Breitkopf und Härtel</a>, n.d.(1903), as part of Hector Berlioz Werke (1900–07), Serie VI, Band XV, edited by Charles Malherbe and Felix Weingartner
</li><li>Kassel: <a href="/wiki/B%C3%A4renreiter" title="Bärenreiter">Bärenreiter</a>, 1975, BA 5453, as part of <a href="/wiki/Hector_Berlioz,_New_Berlioz_Edition" title="Hector Berlioz, New Berlioz Edition" class="mw-redirect">New Berlioz Edition</a> (1967–2005), Volume 13, edited by Ian Kemp
</li></ul>
